Learn the terminology for calculating a bond 's interest payments .
That is to say , the amount you initially loan out , and that you expect to be paid back at the end of the bond 's term .
The end of a bond 's term is known as maturity .
By knowing a bond 's maturity , you can also understand the length of a bond 's term .
A coupon can be thought of as a bond 's interest payment .
A bond 's coupon is typically expressed as a percentage of the bond 's face value .
Distinguish between a bond 's coupon and a bond 's yield .
It is important to know the difference between a bond 's yield , and a bond 's coupon payment in order to not get confused when calculating interest payments .
Sometimes when look at bond 's , you will see both a yield , and a coupon .
For example , the bond 's coupon may be 5 % , and the bond 's coupon may be 10 % .
This is because when calculating a bond 's interest rate , you only need to worry about the coupon .
